This is the "endurance bath" protocol: repeat circulation until the fluid stops changing, then lock it into a final routed container — purification as fixed-point convergence.

### Physics

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[X_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{+,\mathrm{phys}} = P_{\mathrm{P_1}} X_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{-,\mathrm{phys}}, \qquad P_{\mathrm{P_1}} = T_{\mathrm{phys}}^{-1} \Phi_{\mathrm{P_1}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} T_{\mathrm{phys}}\]

  Variable legend: `X^(phys)` tracks containment geometry, phase, pressure, and seal integrity.
  Reading: fluid conduit / circulation command / rotation return line.
  Confidence: strong

- `P.10`
  Equation:

  \[X_{\mathrm{P_10}}^{+,\mathrm{phys}} = P_{\mathrm{P_10}} X_{\mathrm{P_10}}^{-,\mathrm{phys}}, \qquad P_{\mathrm{P_10}} = T_{\mathrm{phys}}^{-1} \Phi_{\mathrm{P_10}}^{\mathrm{AQM}} T_{\mathrm{phys}}\]

### Music Theory and Music Math

- `P.1`
  Equation:

  \[m_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+ = M_{\mathrm{P_1}}m_{\mathrm{P_1}}^-, \qquad \tau_{\mathrm{P_1}} = \|L m_{\mathrm{P_1}}^+\|_2\]

  Variable legend: `m in R^12` is the pitch-tension vector; `tau` is post-line tension.
  Reading: fluid conduit / circulation command / rotation return line.
  Confidence: strong

### Game Theory

- `P.1`

  Variable legend: `y` is the strategy distribution; `R_line` is risk and `C` the control-cost.
  Reading: fluid conduit / circulation command / rotation return line.
  Confidence: strong

## Direct Operational Meaning

This is the "endurance bath" protocol: repeat circulation until the fluid stops changing, then lock it into a final routed container — purification as fixed-point convergence. Process statistics: 56 circulation commands (qo-); 8 valve/clamp checkpoints (ckh/kch); 18 infusion-stabilize cycles (shedy).

## Mathematical Extraction

Across the formal lenses, `f78v` behaves as a fixed-point purification page with N_qo=82, N_valve=12, and N_seal=1. The governing update is x_(n+1) = V(C(x_n)); stop when ||x_(n+1)-x_n|| <= eps, then publish y = S(x_*).

## Mythic Extraction

`f78v` is a bathhouse-laboratory chamber: descend through linked pools, purify by circulation, prove stability at the clamps, and only then carry the living fluid onward.

## All-Lens Zero Point

`This is the "endurance bath" protocol: repeat circulation until the fluid stops changing, then lock it into a final routed container — purification as fixed-point convergence.`

\[\mathcal H := L^2(\widehat{\mathbb C}, \mu), \qquad \rho \in \mathcal T_1(\mathcal H), \qquad \rho \succeq 0, \qquad \mathrm{Tr}(\rho)=1\]

\[\mathcal H_{\mathrm{tot}} = \left(\bigoplus_r \mathcal H_r\right) \oplus \left(\bigoplus_e \mathcal H_{\Lambda_e}\right) \oplus \mathcal H_{\mathrm{fail}}\]

\[x_{n+1}^{\mathrm{chem}} = K_n x_n^{\mathrm{chem}}, \qquad \mathbf{1}^T K_n = \mathbf{1}^T\]

\[g = \mathrm{Coll}(X), \qquad X = \mathrm{Expand}(g) \oplus r\]

\[\Phi_j^{(\lambda)} = T_\lambda^{-1} \circ \Phi_j^{(\mathrm{AQM})} \circ T_\lambda\]

### Typed State Machine

\[
\mathcal R_{f78v} = \{r_{charge}, r_{circulate}, r_{clamp}, r_{commit}, r_{seal}\}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{charge})=r_{circulate}, \qquad
\delta(r_{circulate})=r_{clamp}, \qquad
\delta(r_{clamp})=
\begin{cases}
r_{circulate} & \text{if } \Delta_n > 0 \\
r_{commit} & \text{if } \Delta_n = 0
\end{cases}
\]
\[
\delta(r_{commit})=
\begin{cases}
r_{seal} & \text{if } P_{salt} = 1 \\
r_{circulate} & \text{otherwise}
\end{cases}
\]
